2017-03-12T15:07:00.8917002-04:00 0HL39FBHT341I [INF] Executing action method "blog.Controllers.AuthorController.GetPreviewHtml (blog)" with arguments (["#### Roadmap for 0.2 and 0.3

1. Find all the bugs possible within the features working now and refine until the weekend.
<br />

2. Focus on what to build for the \"0.2\" release -- **Not in order**
    * <strike> Last updated time on blog post needs to be accurate </strike>
    * **Add new post needs to be updated to look like the Edit Post**
    * <strike> Admin shouldn't' take ownership of a post with an author already </strike>
    * **A guide on installing Bagombo on Windows Server 2016 with SQL Express 2016 with IIS**
    * **Ability to make other users and Admin -- this will allow for a Twitter Auth to work as an Admin, kind of skips requiring HTTPS for the login page, for now**
    * A guide to dotnet user-secrets 
    * **Posts need an option to keep them private until they are ready at minimum**
    * **Authors or Admin needs to be able to add categories**
    * **Admin needs to be able to add Features**
    * Authenticated users should be able to add comments
    * Admin needs to be able to delete offensive comments
    * **Authors need to be able to associate a post with categories and a feature(s)**
    * **Author Profile editing**
    * **Features page needs to list features**
    * Recent posts page should list recent posts **OR just remove this page and have recent posts on the home page**
    * Hack together a slow text search for the search tool or remove it for 0.2
    * **All posts page should list all of the posts, separated by month**
    * The 0.2 release will be the first live release on AWS
    * Should be able to change the title of the site
    * Should be able to edit the markdown for inside the JumboTron
    * What to do with the columns below the jumbotron for 0.2
        - 6 Recent Posts
        - Custom posts pointing to:
            * How to edit the columns
            * A guide to markdown
            * A birds eye view of the ASP.NET core and code and how to change things
            * How to change the Site settings page
            * How to install Bagombo
        - 3rd Party Links that will help understand the framework and what it is developed in
            * Markdown
            * Bootstrap
            * ASP.NET Core MVC
            * jQuery
            * C#
        - Author Pages
    * Make the \"Remember Me\" checkbox work

<br />

2. Map out ideas for the \"0.3\" release
    * Upload an image for the author picture - maybe .03
    * When on the edit page, when submit is hit, have the page load with the tab that was last shown at the bottom
    * Facebook Authentication
    * Let Authors download their markdown for personal storage and use
    * Keyboard shortcut to save post on add and edit
    * Better error handling
    * Better logging
    * Pagination
    * Bootstrap Themes
    * Breadcrumbs for site navigation
    * CQS
    * ASP.NET Core community review
